msg:Putian, the second stop of Fujian travel, departs from Fuzhou Intercontinental to Putian Wenjia Wharf early in the morning to take a ferry to Meizhou Island to worship Mazu, and arrives at Putian Shangri-La at 3:00 pm. When entering the lobby, you can smell their unique fragrance. The lobby decoration is exquisite There are Fujian style and a little Japanese style, the overall hardware design is very careful and meticulous, the room is small, low-key luxury, decorated with a lot of wood grain, the service staff is very good, not the enthusiasm from the show kind, but they all answered my questions patiently with a shy expression, which is great.
There are not many types of breakfast, but the presentation is exquisite and thoughtful, the taste is also very good, the dining environment is also very comfortable, the gym facilities are very complete, the swimming pool is very clean and there are very few people.
Although the hotel is a bit far from the city center, it is a good deal to spend an extra 20 yuan for an online car-hailing car to go to Xinghua Prefecture.
Although they are all very good, I still have to complain about two things. When I checked in, I told that I needed to add Shangri-La membership points. The supervisor at the counter told me that I couldn‚Äôt have points because I booked with Ctrip. I didn‚Äôt understand. In addition, many people said in the comments that the hotel will upgrade the room to a lake-view room. I saw that there were very few guests staying in the hotel that day. I may be sorry for my long face. The floor given to me was very low and faced the main road. In most five-star hotels, if there are not many guests, I will arrange an upgrade, not to mention that I am a member of them and a diamond member of Ctrip. I was upgraded at the InterContinental in Fuzhou the day before.
One last thing, Ctrip told me that the check-out time is 2:00 pm, and there was a piece of paper in the room card that said check-out was at 12:00 noon, so I asked her, and the system only said yes after checking.
